*2021 Chrism Mass summary from meetings*

Due to Covid restrictions. The following will apply.

1. *Atendance* 
a. ONLY Priests and religious.
b. Selected members of the Laity (2  per deanery, and selected reps of select Archdiocesan Groups). The 2 committee members will represent their parishes.

2. *Lay and others participation*

a. On TV via
- *LUMEN CHRISTI DSTV channel 350* and *GOTV Channel 29*

b. Online Streaming will be available on: *www.chrismmasslagos.com* 

3. *Dates and Time of event*

Badagry region:
*Tuesday 30th March* @  *9am*

Holy Cross Cathedral:
*Thursday 1st April* @  *9am*

4. *Gifts for the Archbishop*
Deans are to coordinate and arrange to send to the chancery, preferably before the Chrism Mass.
